Run cd $OPENWRT_PATH
  cd $OPENWRT_PATH
  echo "开始编译软件包，使用 $(nproc) 线程"
  make diffconfig
  # 编译acctl软件包，启用详细输出
  echo "编译acctl软件包"
  make package/acctl/compile V=99 || {
    echo "acctl编译失败，尝试单线程编译"
    make package/acctl/compile -j1 V=s
  }
  # 生成软件包索引
  echo "生成软件包索引"
  make package/index
  shell: /usr/bin/bash -e {0}
